SECTION: Application Security And Logging
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 1
A company's web application, running behind an Application Load Balancer, has been targeted by a series of SQL injection attacks. Which AWS service is specifically designed to mitigate this type of threat?

A. AWS Shield Advanced
B. AWS WAF
C. Network ACLs
D. Security Groups

Answer: B

---

Question #: 2
An administrator needs to find out who terminated a specific EC2 instance last week. Which AWS service provides a log of all API calls made in the account, including the identity of the caller?

A. Amazon CloudWatch Logs
B. VPC Flow Logs
C. AWS CloudTrail
D. AWS Config

Answer: C

---

Question #: 3
You want to receive an email notification whenever the CPU Utilization of a critical EC2 instance exceeds 80% for 5 consecutive minutes. Which combination of services should you use? (Choose TWO)

A. AWS CloudTrail
B. Amazon CloudWatch Metrics
C. AWS Shield
D. Amazon Simple Notification Service (SNS)
E. AWS Lambda

Answer: B, D

---

Question #: 4
A gaming company is preparing for a major online game launch and anticipates large-scale, sophisticated DDoS attacks. They require 24/7 access to the AWS DDoS Response Team (DRT) for assistance during an attack. Which service should they subscribe to?

A. AWS Shield Standard
B. AWS WAF with a rate-based rule
C. AWS Shield Advanced
D. Amazon GuardDuty

Answer: C

---

Question #: 5
A solutions architect wants to block web traffic from a specific country known for malicious activity. How can this be configured using AWS WAF?

A. By creating a custom rule with an IP set condition.
B. By using a managed rule group for geographic blocking.
C. By creating a geographic match rule.
D. By configuring a rate-based rule.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 6
Which of the following is a feature of AWS Shield Standard?

A. Protection against application layer DDoS attacks (e.g., HTTP floods).
B. Access to the AWS DDoS Response Team (DRT).
C. DDoS cost protection for scaling charges.
D. Automatic protection against common network and transport layer DDoS attacks.

Answer: D

---

Question #: 7
A security team wants to ensure that all API activity within their AWS account is logged and the log files are encrypted and cannot be tampered with. Which feature of AWS CloudTrail should they enable?

A. CloudTrail Insights
B. Event History
C. Log File Integrity Validation
D. Management Events logging

Answer: C

---

Question #: 8
An application running on EC2 instances generates custom log files. The operations team wants to centralize these logs for analysis and set up alarms based on specific error patterns (e.g., "ERROR_500"). What is the best approach?

A. Store logs in S3 and use Amazon Athena for queries.
B. Install the CloudWatch Logs agent on the EC2 instances to stream logs to CloudWatch Logs.
C. Write a custom script to periodically push logs to an Amazon SQS queue.
D. Enable VPC Flow Logs for the EC2 instances' ENIs.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 9
What is the primary function of a Web ACL in AWS WAF?

A. To define a set of AWS resources that you want to protect.
B. To contain a collection of rules that are evaluated for web requests.
C. To monitor, filter, and block DNS queries.
D. To provide detailed logs of all allowed web traffic.

Answer: B

Question #: 10

A. Amazon DynamoDB
B. Amazon S3
C. Amazon CloudWatch Logs
D. Amazon Kinesis Data Streams

Question #: 11
A company is using an Application Load Balancer (ALB). They want to allow all traffic by default but explicitly block a list of malicious IP addresses. What is the correct configuration in their AWS WAF Web ACL?

A. Set the default action to ALLOW and create a rule with an IP set match condition that has its action set to BLOCK.
B. Set the default action to BLOCK and create a rule with an IP set match condition that has its action set to ALLOW.
C. Create two rules: one to allow all traffic and another to block the specific IP addresses.
D. Configure the ALB's security group to deny the malicious IP addresses.

Answer: A

Which of the following is NOT a valid target for a CloudWatch Events rule (EventBridge)?

A. AWS Lambda function
B. Amazon SQS queue
C. Amazon S3 bucket
D. SNS topic

Answer: C

---

Question #: 84
A security audit requires a report of every IAM user who has logged into the AWS console in the last 30 days. Which service provides this information?

A. AWS Config
B. Amazon CloudWatch
C. AWS CloudTrail
D. IAM Credential Report

Answer: C

---

Question #: 85
Which service provides automated, managed protection for your AWS resources against Distributed Denial of Service (DDoS) attacks?

A. AWS WAF
B. Amazon Inspector
C. AWS Shield
D. Network ACLs

Answer: C

---

Question #: 86
You have set up a CloudWatch alarm that sends a notification to an SNS topic. The SNS topic has an email subscriber. The subscriber has received the confirmation email but has not yet confirmed the subscription. What will happen when the alarm is triggered?

A. The email will be sent to the subscriber.
B. The alarm will fail to trigger the SNS action.
C. The email will not be sent to that specific subscriber, but other confirmed subscribers will receive it.
D. The SNS topic will be automatically deleted.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 87
What is the primary goal of enabling log file integrity validation for AWS CloudTrail?

A. To encrypt the log files.
B. To determine if a log file was modified, deleted, or unchanged after CloudTrail delivered it.
C. To compress the log files to save space.
D. To validate the format of the log files.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 88
A company wants to block requests that appear to be a command injection attack (e.g., contains `/bin/bash`). Which AWS service should be used?

A. AWS Shield
B. A Security Group
C. An AWS WAF Managed Rule Group for Linux attacks
D. A Network ACL

Answer: C

---

Question #: 89
What is a CloudWatch Log Stream?

A. A sequence of log events that share the same source.
B. A real-time feed of metrics from an AWS service.
C. A query used in CloudWatch Logs Insights.
D. A filter that extracts metric data from logs.

Answer: A

---

Question #: 90
Can CloudTrail log API calls made from the AWS CLI and AWS SDKs?

A. No, it only logs calls made from the AWS Management Console.
B. Yes, it logs API calls from any source, including the console, CLI, and SDKs.
C. It only logs calls made from the CLI, not the SDKs.
D. It only logs calls that result in a change to a resource.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 91
What happens if a web request matches a rule with a "BLOCK" action in a Web ACL?

A. The request is allowed, but an alert is logged in CloudWatch.
B. AWS WAF responds with a 403 (Forbidden) HTTP status code and does not forward the request to the resource.
C. The request is forwarded to the resource, but with a special header indicating it should be blocked.
D. The source IP address of the request is permanently added to a denylist.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 92
You are troubleshooting an issue and want to view the last few minutes of log data from a Lambda function. Where would you look?

A. In the AWS CloudTrail Event History.
B. In the Amazon CloudWatch Logs console, within the log group for that function.
C. In the VPC Flow Logs for the VPC where the function is running.
D. On the Lambda function's "Monitoring" tab, which shows CloudTrail events.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 93
Which of the following is an example of a CloudTrail management event?

A. An S3 `GetObject` request.
B. A Lambda function invocation.
C. An EC2 `RunInstances` API call.
D. A DynamoDB `GetItem` request.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 94
If you associate a Web ACL with an ALB, what happens to the logs for requests that are blocked by AWS WAF?

A. They are not logged anywhere.
B. They appear in the ALB access logs with a `WAF-Blocked` status.
C. They are sent to AWS CloudTrail automatically.
D. They can be configured to be sent to CloudWatch Logs, S3, or Kinesis Data Firehose.

Answer: D

---

Question #: 95
A composite alarm in Amazon CloudWatch is an alarm that...

A. monitors multiple metrics at the same time.
B. can take multiple actions when it is triggered.
C. combines the states of several other alarms into an overall state.
D. is created using a combination of AWS services.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 96
AWS WAF is considered a regional service, with one exception. When used with which service does AWS WAF become a global service?

A. Amazon API Gateway
B. Application Load Balancer
C. Amazon CloudFront
D. AWS AppSync

Answer: C

---

Question #: 97
You need to ensure that CloudTrail is enabled in all existing and future AWS accounts within your AWS Organization. What is the most efficient way to manage this?

A. Manually create a trail in each member account.
B. Use AWS CloudFormation StackSets to deploy a trail to all accounts.
C. Create an AWS Organization trail from the management account.
D. Write a script that uses the AWS CLI to create trails in each account.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 98

A. AWS CloudTrail
B. Amazon CloudWatch
C. AWS Personal Health Dashboard
D. AWS Cost Explorer

Answer: B

---

Question #: 99
A security team wants to prevent developers from accidentally making an S3 bucket public. They can use AWS Config to detect this, but what service can be used to log the `PutBucketAcl` API call that made the bucket public?

A. VPC Flow Logs
B. AWS Shield
C. S3 Server Access Logs
D. AWS CloudTrail

Answer: D

---

Question #: 100
An application is experiencing an attack where requests are malformed and contain attempts to exploit a known vulnerability in a popular content management system. What is the BEST way to block this specific exploit without impacting legitimate traffic?

A. Block the IP addresses of the attackers.
B. Use a Security Group to restrict access to the application.
C. Use a specific rule from an AWS Managed Rule Group in WAF that targets that CMS's vulnerabilities.
D. Use AWS Shield Standard to mitigate the attack.

Answer: C

B. IAM Group
C. IAM Role
D. Access Keys
E. IAM Policy

Answer: C

Question #: 102
An IAM user must manage only Amazon S3 buckets. Which action will achieve the principle of least privilege?

A. Attach AdministratorAccess policy
B. Attach AmazonS3FullAccess policy
C. Attach a custom policy allowing only s3:* actions
D. Make the user part of the PowerUser group

Answer: C

Question #: 103
Which TWO are true about IAM policies? (Choose TWO)

A. Policies can be attached to groups
B. Policies can be attached to IAM roles
C. Policies can be attached directly to EC2 instances
D. Policies can deny as well as allow access
E. Policies cannot be attached to IAM users

Answer: A,B,D

SECTION: Cost-Optimized Compute And Storage
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 201
A company runs a critical database on an EC2 instance 24/7. The workload is very stable and predictable. To achieve the highest possible discount on compute costs for this instance, which EC2 purchasing option should be used?

A. Spot Instances
B. On-Demand Instances
C. Standard Reserved Instances (3-year term, all upfront payment)
D. Dedicated Hosts

Answer: C

---

Question #: 202
An application writes log files to an Amazon S3 bucket. The logs are actively analyzed for the first 30 days, then accessed infrequently for another 60 days for troubleshooting. After 90 days, they must be archived for 7 years for compliance. What is the most cost-effective S3 lifecycle policy configuration?

A. Transition to S3 Standard-IA after 30 days, then to S3 Glacier Deep Archive after 90 days.
B. Transition to S3 Intelligent-Tiering after 30 days, then expire after 90 days.
C. Transition to S3 One Zone-IA after 30 days, then to S3 Glacier Flexible Retrieval after 365 days.
D. Keep in S3 Standard for 90 days, then transition to S3 Glacier Deep Archive.

Answer: A

---

Question #: 203
A company runs large-scale data processing jobs that can be interrupted and resumed at any time. The primary goal is to minimize the cost of the EC2 instances used for this workload. Which purchasing option offers the largest discounts but comes with the risk of termination?

A. On-Demand Instances
B. Savings Plans
C. Reserved Instances
D. Spot Instances

Answer: D

---

Question #: 204
A company has a large amount of data in Amazon S3 that is accessed unpredictably. Some data is accessed frequently for a few months, then not at all. They want to automate cost savings without needing to analyze access patterns manually. Which S3 storage class is designed for this use case?

A. S3 Standard
B. S3 Standard-Infrequent Access (IA)
C. S3 Intelligent-Tiering
D. S3 Glacier Flexible Retrieval

Answer: C

---

Question #: 205
A company has committed to a consistent amount of compute usage (e.g., $10/hour) across a variety of instance families and regions. They want a flexible pricing model that offers a discount in exchange for this commitment, without being locked into a specific instance type. Which purchasing option is the best fit?

A. Standard Reserved Instances
B. Convertible Reserved Instances
C. Compute Savings Plans
D. Spot Instances

Answer: C

---

Question #: 206
A company needs to store data that is critical and frequently accessed, but only exists in a single Availability Zone. To save costs, they are willing to accept the risk that the data would be lost if that AZ fails. Which S3 storage class is designed for this scenario?

A. S3 Standard
B. S3 Standard-Infrequent Access (IA)
C. S3 One Zone-Infrequent Access (IA)
D. S3 Glacier Instant Retrieval

Answer: C

---

Question #: 207
A company has purchased a 1-year, All Upfront, Standard Reserved Instance for an m5.large instance. After 6 months, they realize they no longer need the instance. What can they do to recoup some of the cost of the unused reservation?

A. Cancel the Reserved Instance and receive a pro-rated refund from AWS.
B. Sell the Reserved Instance on the AWS Reserved Instance Marketplace.
C. Exchange the m5.large reservation for a t3.micro reservation.
D. Nothing, the cost is sunk and cannot be recovered.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 208
An S3 lifecycle policy is configured to transition objects to S3 Glacier Flexible Retrieval after 60 days. An object is 1 byte in size. What is a potential issue with this configuration?

A. S3 Glacier has a minimum storage duration charge (e.g., 90 days).
B. There may be an overhead charge for metadata and indexing for small objects in S3 Glacier.
C. S3 Glacier cannot store objects smaller than 128 KB.
D. Both A and B are potential issues.

Answer: D

---

Question #: 209
What is a key difference between a Standard Reserved Instance and a Convertible Reserved Instance?

A. Convertible RIs offer a larger discount than Standard RIs.
B. Standard RIs can be sold on the marketplace, while Convertible RIs cannot.
C. Convertible RIs can be exchanged for another RI with different attributes (like instance family or OS) of equal or greater value.
D. Standard RIs are paid for monthly, while Convertible RIs must be paid for all upfront.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 210
An application archives data to S3 Glacier Deep Archive for long-term retention. A compliance audit requires that a specific 100 GB file be retrieved within 8 hours. What is the most cost-effective retrieval option?

A. Expedited Retrieval
B. Standard Retrieval
C. Bulk Retrieval
D. This is not possible; Deep Archive retrieval takes at least 12 hours.

Answer: B (Standard retrieval from Deep Archive is within 12 hours, but this is the "standard" option available).

---

Question #: 211
A company uses a large number of EC2 instances for a stateless web application. The instances can be terminated and replaced without affecting the application's availability. The workload runs 24/7 but can tolerate interruptions. To optimize costs, the company uses a fleet of Spot Instances. How can they reduce the impact of Spot Instance terminations?

A. Use a Spot Fleet configured to request instances across multiple instance types and Availability Zones.
B. Request a very high Spot price.
C. Use Reserved Instances as a backup.
D. Only run the workload during off-peak hours.

Answer: A

---

Question #: 212
An S3 lifecycle policy is configured with the following rule: Transition objects to S3 Standard-IA after 30 days. An object is uploaded and then deleted 15 days later. How will the S3 charges be affected?

A. There will be no extra charge.
B. The object will still be billed for the full 30 days of S3 Standard-IA storage due to the minimum storage duration.
C. A pro-rated early delete fee for S3 Standard-IA will be charged.
D. The lifecycle policy will fail to run.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 213
Which purchasing option provides a discount on EC2 usage in exchange for a 1- or 3-year commitment to a consistent amount of usage, measured in $/hour?

A. Spot Instances
B. On-Demand Instances
C. Savings Plans
D. Pay-as-you-go

Answer: C

---

Question #: 214
A company needs to store medical images that are accessed infrequently but must be available for retrieval in milliseconds when requested by a doctor. Which S3 storage class is the most cost-effective for this use case?

A. S3 Standard
B. S3 Standard-Infrequent Access (IA)
C. S3 Glacier Flexible Retrieval
D. S3 Glacier Instant Retrieval

Answer: D

---

Question #: 215
An EC2 instance is launched using the On-Demand purchasing option. How is the instance billed?

A. By the month, with a fixed fee.
B. By the hour or by the second (depending on the instance type and OS), with no long-term commitment.
C. A one-time upfront payment for a 1-year term.
D. Based on the current Spot market price.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 216
What is the primary purpose of an S3 lifecycle policy?

A. To automatically version objects in a bucket.
B. To automate the process of moving objects between S3 storage classes or expiring them to save costs.
C. To replicate objects to another AWS Region for disaster recovery.
D. To encrypt all new objects added to a bucket.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 217

A. Standard Reserved Instances
B. Dedicated Hosts
C. Spot Blocks
D. Capacity Reservations

Answer: B

---

Question #: 218
An object is stored in S3 Intelligent-Tiering. It is accessed every day for two months, and then it is not accessed again for three months. How will S3 Intelligent-Tiering handle this object?

A. It will remain in the Frequent Access tier for the entire five months.
B. It will start in the Frequent Access tier, and after 30 consecutive days of no access, it will be automatically moved to the Infrequent Access tier.
C. It will start in the Frequent Access tier and be moved to S3 Glacier Deep Archive after 90 days.
D. The user must manually transition the object between tiers.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 219
Which of the following is a benefit of a Compute Savings Plan over a Standard Reserved Instance?

A. It provides a higher discount.
B. It is more flexible; the discount applies automatically to any EC2 instance usage up to the commitment, regardless of instance family, size, OS, or region.
C. It can be sold on a marketplace.
D. It has a shorter commitment term (6 months).

Answer: B

Question #: 220

D. 12-24 hours

Question #: 222

B. The time since the object was created.
C. The time since the lifecycle rule was created.
D. The time since the object was last modified.

Answer: B

Question #: 223

Question #: 224

C. Deep Archive does not support lifecycle policies.
D. Deep Archive has lower durability than Flexible Retrieval.

Question #: 225

A. It provides a discount on any EC2 instance usage globally.
B. It provides the highest discount in exchange for a commitment to a specific instance family in a specific region (e.g., m5 in us-east-1).
C. It allows you to bid on spare EC2 capacity.

B. Create two lifecycle rules, one for the transition and one for the size filter.
C. This is not possible; lifecycle rules cannot filter by object size.

Question #: 236

C. The current version receives a delete marker, becoming a previous version, and is not yet permanently deleted.

Question #: 245

C. You will receive an error message.
D. The instance will be launched and then immediately terminated.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 246
A lifecycle policy has two conflicting rules: one that transitions objects to S3-IA after 30 days and another that transitions them to S3 Glacier after 60 days. An object is 70 days old. Where will it be stored?

A. S3 Standard
B. S3-IA
C. S3 Glacier
D. The outcome is unpredictable.

Answer: C (Lifecycle rules are evaluated, and the action for the longer period takes effect).

---

Question #: 247
Which of the following is true about On-Demand Capacity Reservations?

A. They provide a discount on EC2 instance costs.

Question #: 252

Question #: 253
A lifecycle policy is configured to transition objects to S3 Glacier Deep Archive. What is the minimum number of days an object must be stored in S3 Standard before it can be transitioned to Deep Archive?

A. 0 days
B. 30 days
C. 90 days
D. 180 days

Answer: A (There's no minimum storage time in Standard before transition, but there is a minimum charge in the destination class).

Question #: 259

Question #: 260
An S3 object has been in the S3 Intelligent-Tiering class for a year without being accessed. Which of the optional archive tiers might it have been moved to automatically? (Choose TWO)

A. S3 Glacier Instant Retrieval
B. S3 Glacier Flexible Retrieval
C. S3 Glacier Deep Archive
D. S3 Standard-IA
E. S3 One Zone-IA

Answer: B, C (If the optional async archive access tiers are enabled).

Question #: 282

B. An S3 lifecycle policy based on the creation date.
C. S3 Storage Lens to identify cold data.
D. S3 Intelligent-Tiering, which handles this automatically.

Answer: A (This is a trick question. Standard S3 lifecycle policies work on creation time, not last-access time. S3-IT is the service that does this automatically).

Question #: 299
A lifecycle policy is set to expire objects 1 day after creation. An object is uploaded at 10:00 AM on Monday. When will the object be deleted?

A. At 10:01 AM on Monday.
B. At 10:01 AM on Tuesday.
C. At midnight on Tuesday (transitioning from Tuesday to Wednesday).
D. The exact time is not guaranteed but will be after 24 hours have passed.

Answer: C (Lifecycle policies run once a day, around midnight UTC, so the object will be deleted after it has been 1 day old when the policy runs).

Answer: B

Question #: 302
A developer is optimizing a Lambda function and notices that increasing the memory from 128 MB to 256 MB significantly decreases the execution time. How does this memory change affect the overall cost of the Lambda function?

A. The cost will always increase because the per-millisecond rate is higher for more memory.
B. The cost will always decrease because the execution time is shorter.
C. The cost may increase, decrease, or stay the same, depending on whether the reduction in duration outweighs the increase in the per-millisecond price.
D. The cost is only based on the number of invocations, so the memory change has no effect.

Answer: C

D. Decrease the visibility timeout of the queue.

Question #: 357
How does using a Lambda Layer with a common dependency (e.g., the AWS SDK) potentially save costs?

A. It reduces the size of the function's deployment package, which can speed up deployments.
B. It does not directly save costs but improves performance.
C. Lambda Layers are billed at a lower rate than function code.
D. It reduces the number of required invocations.

Answer: A (While not a direct cost saving, smaller packages can lead to faster cold starts, which slightly reduces duration costs over many invocations).

SECTION: Data Encryption Questions
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 401
Which AWS service is primarily used for creating and managing encryption keys?

A. AWS Secrets Manager
B. AWS Certificate Manager
C. AWS KMS
D. Amazon Cognito

Answer: C

Question #: 402
Which TWO statements about AWS KMS are correct? (Choose TWO)

A. KMS keys can be customer-managed
B. KMS supports automatic key rotation
C. KMS can only encrypt objects larger than 4 KB directly
D. KMS integrates with S3, EBS, and RDS
E. KMS is only available in a single AWS region

Answer: A,B,D

Question #: 403
How does Amazon S3 provide encryption at rest?

A. Using AWS KMS-managed keys (SSE-KMS)
B. Using server-side encryption with Amazon S3-managed keys (SSE-S3)
C. Using client-side encryption
D. All of the above

Answer: D

Question #: 404
Which TWO are valid methods for encrypting Amazon EBS volumes? (Choose TWO)

A. Enable EBS encryption when creating a volume
B. Encrypt the root volume after EC2 instance launch without downtime
C. Copy an unencrypted snapshot to an encrypted snapshot
D. Attach an IAM role with encryption permissions
E. Use an external VPN tunnel

Answer: A,C

Question #: 405
Which is the best practice for encrypting RDS databases at rest?

A. Enable encryption when creating the RDS instance
B. Enable SSL connections
C. Attach a Security Group
D. Configure IAM roles

Answer: A

Question #: 406
Which TWO methods can be used to encrypt data in transit to an Amazon RDS database? (Choose TWO)

A. Use SSL/TLS connections
B. Enable IAM authentication
C. Encrypt the storage layer
D. Configure client applications to require SSL
E. Attach a KMS key directly to SQL queries

Answer: A,D

Question #: 407
Which statement is true about SSL/TLS encryption in AWS?

A. It only applies to S3
B. It encrypts data in transit between clients and services
C. It encrypts data at rest automatically
D. It replaces IAM policies

Answer: B

Question #: 408

A. Amazon S3
B. Amazon EC2
C. Amazon EBS
D. Amazon Route 53
E. AWS Lambda

Answer: A,C

D. AWS Secrets Manager

SECTION: Decoupled Architectures
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 501
An application processes user-uploaded images by placing a job in an Amazon SQS queue. A fleet of EC2 instances polls the queue to perform the processing. The processing for each image can take up to 10 minutes. What should a solutions architect do to prevent the same image from being processed by multiple instances simultaneously?

A. Increase the number of EC2 instances polling the queue.
B. Configure the SQS queue's Visibility Timeout to be greater than 10 minutes.
C. Use an SQS FIFO queue instead of a Standard queue.
D. Set the Message Retention Period to 10 minutes.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 502
A company has a microservices architecture where multiple, independent backend services need to be notified whenever a new customer signs up. The number of services that need this notification is expected to grow. What is the most scalable and decoupled way to distribute the "new customer" event?

A. The customer service should directly call an API endpoint on each interested backend service.
B. The customer service should publish a message to an Amazon SNS topic, and each backend service should subscribe to that topic.
C. The customer service should write the event to an SQS queue, which all backend services poll.
D. The customer service should write the event to a DynamoDB table, and all services should scan the table for new entries.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 503
A Lambda function is configured with an SQS standard queue as its event source. The function processes messages and sometimes experiences transient errors, causing it to fail. What happens to a message if the Lambda function execution fails for that message?

A. The message is permanently deleted from the queue.
B. The message is sent to a dead-letter queue (DLQ), if one is configured.
C. The message becomes visible in the queue again after the visibility timeout expires and can be processed again.
D. The SQS queue is automatically disabled.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 504
An order processing system needs to ensure that orders are processed in the exact sequence they are received and that no duplicate orders are processed. Which AWS service and feature should be used?

A. Amazon SQS Standard Queue
B. Amazon SNS Topic
C. Amazon SQS FIFO (First-In, First-Out) Queue
D. AWS Lambda with a concurrency limit of 1

Answer: C

---

Question #: 505
An SNS topic has three subscribers: an SQS queue, an AWS Lambda function, and an HTTPS endpoint. When a message is published to the topic, what is the expected behavior?

A. SNS will send the message to only one of the subscribers, chosen at random.
B. SNS will send the message to the SQS queue first, then the Lambda function, then the HTTPS endpoint.
C. SNS will attempt to deliver a copy of the message to all three subscribers in parallel.
D. SNS will queue the message and wait for each subscriber to poll for it.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 506
A developer is using an SQS FIFO queue and notices that message processing has stalled. No new messages are being received, even though the queue is not empty. What is the most likely cause?

A. The Visibility Timeout is set too low.
B. A message with a specific Message Group ID is being processed, and all other messages in that same group are blocked until the first one is successfully processed and deleted.
C. The SQS queue has reached its maximum message limit.
D. The IAM permissions for the consumer are incorrect.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 507
A company wants to send promotional emails to customers, but also send push notifications to customers who have the mobile app installed. The message content for email and the mobile push notification needs to be different. How can this be achieved with a single SNS publish action?

A. Publish two separate messages to the same topic.
B. Use an SQS queue to transform the message before sending it.
C. Publish a JSON message with different structures for each delivery protocol (e.g., `default`, `email`, `APNS`).
D. This is not possible; a separate SNS topic is needed for each message format.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 508
What is the primary architectural benefit of decoupling an application's components using a message queue like Amazon SQS?

A. It increases the performance of individual components.
B. It improves reliability by allowing components to fail independently without causing the entire system to fail.
C. It reduces the cost of data transfer between components.
D. It simplifies the application's code by combining components into a monolith.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 509
An SQS queue is configured with a dead-letter queue (DLQ). Under what condition is a message sent to the DLQ?

A. When the queue is full.
B. When a consumer successfully processes the message.
C. After a consumer fails to process the message a specified number of times (the `maxReceiveCount`).
D. When the message's visibility timeout expires.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 510
An SNS topic needs to send notifications only to subscribers that are interested in certain types of events. For example, some subscribers only want to know about "order_created" events, while others only want "order_shipped" events. How can this be implemented?

A. Use multiple SNS topics, one for each event type.
B. Publish all events to one topic and let the subscribers filter the messages on their end.
C. Use SNS subscription filter policies to deliver messages based on message attributes.
D. Use an SQS queue as a buffer to filter messages before they are published.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 511
What is the default message retention period for an Amazon SQS queue?

A. 1 minute
B. 1 hour
C. 4 days
D. 14 days

Answer: C

---

Question #: 512
A Lambda function is triggered by messages in an SQS queue. The function needs more than the default 3 seconds to process each message. The function is timing out and causing messages to be reprocessed. What should the developer do? (Choose TWO)

A. Increase the Lambda function's memory allocation.
B. Increase the SQS queue's Visibility Timeout to be longer than the Lambda function's timeout.
C. Increase the Lambda function's timeout setting.
D. Use an SQS FIFO queue instead of a Standard queue.
E. Decrease the batch size of the Lambda event source mapping.

Answer: B, C

---

Question #: 513
An application publishes sensitive messages to an SNS topic. What is the best way to ensure the messages are encrypted at rest within the SNS service?

A. Encrypt the messages in the application before publishing them.
B. Enable server-side encryption (SSE) on the SNS topic using an AWS KMS key.
C. Ensure all subscribers use HTTPS endpoints.
D. This is the default behavior; all SNS messages are encrypted at rest.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 514
An SQS queue uses short polling. What is the behavior of the consumer when it makes a `ReceiveMessage` API call and the queue is empty?

A. The call waits for a specified time for messages to arrive.
B. The call immediately returns an empty response.
C. The call returns an error.
D. The call is charged as a full request even if no message is returned.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 515
Which of the following is a valid subscriber type for an Amazon SNS topic? (Choose TWO)

A. Amazon EC2 Instance
B. AWS Lambda function
C. Amazon SQS queue
D. Amazon DynamoDB table
E. An S3 bucket

Answer: B, C

---

Question #: 516
A company wants to reduce costs associated with its SQS usage. Their application has consumers that are constantly polling a queue, even when it is often empty. Which SQS feature should they use to reduce the number of empty responses and lower costs?

A. Dead-Letter Queue (DLQ)
B. Visibility Timeout
C. Long Polling
D. Message Timers

Answer: C

---

Question #: 517
A fan-out architecture is a common design pattern in event-driven systems. Which combination of AWS services is ideal for implementing this pattern?

A. An SQS queue with multiple consumers.
B. An SNS topic with multiple SQS queue subscriptions.
C. A single Lambda function that calls multiple other Lambda functions.
D. A DynamoDB table with multiple Global Secondary Indexes.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 518
A Lambda function needs to process batches of up to 10 messages at a time from an SQS queue. How should this be configured?

A. In the Lambda function's code, make 10 `ReceiveMessage` calls.
B. In the SQS queue settings, set the maximum batch size to 10.
C. In the Lambda event source mapping configuration, set the Batch Size to 10.
D. This is the default behavior and requires no configuration.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 519
What is the maximum size of a message that can be sent to Amazon SQS or Amazon SNS?

A. 64 KB
B. 256 KB
C. 1 MB
D. 2 GB

Answer: B

---

Question #: 520
A solutions architect is designing a system where a message must be processed by one component, and then a notification about the completion must be sent to multiple other components. Which architecture best fits this use case?

A. A single SNS topic for both processing and notifications.
B. An SQS queue for the initial processing, with the processing component then publishing a completion message to an SNS topic.
C. A single SQS queue that all components poll.
D. An SNS topic that triggers a Lambda function, which then writes to an SQS queue.

Question #: 576
A Lambda function processes messages from an SQS queue. The function is observed to be running constantly, even when there are no messages, leading to high costs. What is the most likely misconfiguration?

A. The SQS queue is not configured for long polling, causing the Lambda service to poll very rapidly.
B. The Lambda function has a memory leak.
C. The visibility timeout of the queue is set to 0.
D. The Lambda function's timeout is set too high.

Answer: A (This behavior is more typical of self-polling applications, but in the context of Lambda's polling, a lack of long polling can lead to more invocations, some of which may be empty). *A more accurate answer might be a misconfigured wait time in the event source mapping, but A is the closest concept.*

Question #: 590

A. Amazon SQS
B. Amazon SNS
C. Amazon EventBridge
D. Amazon Kinesis

Answer: C

---

Question #: 591
When using an SQS FIFO queue, what is the maximum throughput (API calls per second) it can support by default in most regions?

A. 300 messages per second.
B. 3,000 messages per second (or 300 API calls with batching).
C. 10,000 messages per second.
D. Unlimited.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 592
A Lambda function processes sensitive data and is invoked by an S3 event. The security team requires a full audit trail of every time the function is invoked, including the invoker's identity. Which service provides this?

A. Amazon CloudWatch Logs
B. AWS X-Ray
C. AWS CloudTrail (by logging the S3 event that invoked the function)
D. VPC Flow Logs

Answer: C

---

Question #: 593
Which service is most appropriate for a scenario where you need to buffer a massive, real-time stream of data (e.g., clickstream data from a website) before it is loaded into a data warehouse?

A. Amazon SQS
B. Amazon SNS
C. Amazon Kinesis Data Firehose
D. AWS Step Functions

Answer: C

---

Question #: 594
A message is published to an SNS topic, which fans out to 5 SQS queues. How many times is the user billed for the SNS publish action?

A. Once for the publish to the topic.
B. Six times (once for the publish and once for each of the 5 deliveries).
C. Five times (once for each delivery).
D. The publish action is free; only the deliveries are billed.

Answer: A (Publish actions are billable, as are deliveries. The question asks about the publish action itself).

---

Question #: 595
To achieve decoupling, a web server needs to send a job to a backend processor. The web server does not need to wait for a reply. This is an example of what kind of communication?

A. Synchronous communication
B. Asynchronous communication
C. Stateful communication
D. Request/Response communication

Answer: B

---

Question #: 596
An SQS message consumer needs to process a message for 20 minutes. The SQS queue's maximum visibility timeout is 12 hours. What is a potential problem with this design?

A. The message will be deleted before processing is finished.
B. The consumer might be considered "stuck" and the message may not be re-processed in case of a real failure. This long processing time is better suited for a different pattern, like Step Functions.
C. The SQS queue will not allow a timeout this long.
D. The cost of the SQS queue will be excessively high.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 597
What is the primary function of Amazon EventBridge?

A. To provide long-term, ordered storage for event records.
B. To act as a serverless, event-driven integration service that connects application components with data from various sources.
C. To guarantee the processing order of events.
D. To provide a simple pub/sub messaging service for high-throughput notifications.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 598
A company wants to send a one-time password (OTP) to a user's mobile phone via SMS as part of a multi-factor authentication system. Which service is most suitable for sending the SMS message?

A. Amazon SQS
B. Amazon SNS
C. AWS Lambda
D. Amazon Pinpoint

Answer: B (or D, as Pinpoint is also for user engagement, but SNS is the direct service for SMS).

---

Question #: 599
A developer uses the `ChangeMessageVisibility` call to extend the timeout for a message in an SQS queue. What is a key limitation of this call?

A. It can only be called once per message.
B. It can only shorten the timeout, not extend it.
C. It requires special IAM permissions that are not granted by default.
D. It can only extend the timeout up to the queue's configured maximum visibility timeout (max 12 hours).

Answer: D

---

Question #: 600
Which of the following represents the most decoupled architecture?

A. A monolithic application where all components are in a single codebase.
B. A microservices architecture where services communicate with each other via synchronous REST API calls.
C. A microservices architecture where services communicate by publishing and subscribing to events on a message bus like SNS or EventBridge.
D. A two-tier architecture with a web server directly writing to a relational database.

Answer: C


SECTION: Disaster Decovery Questions
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 601
A company has defined a Recovery Time Objective (RTO) of 2 hours. What does this mean for their disaster recovery plan?

A. The company can tolerate losing up to 2 hours of data in a disaster.
B. The entire system must be fully operational within 2 hours of a disaster declaration.
C. Backups must be taken every 2 hours.
D. The disaster recovery site must be located in a region that is a 2-hour flight away.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 602
A financial services firm has a Recovery Point Objective (RPO) of 15 minutes for its critical transaction database. What does this requirement imply?

A. The system must be restored within 15 minutes of a failure.
B. The maximum acceptable amount of data loss is 15 minutes' worth of transactions.
C. The database failover process must complete in under 15 minutes.
D. Database snapshots must be retained for at least 15 minutes.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 603
A company is implementing a disaster recovery strategy with the lowest possible cost. They have an RTO of 24 hours and an RPO of 12 hours. Which DR strategy is the most appropriate and cost-effective?

A. Warm Standby
B. Multi-site Active-Active
C. Pilot Light
D. Backup and Restore

Answer: D

---

Question #: 604
In a Backup and Restore disaster recovery strategy for an application running on EC2 instances, what AWS services are typically used to store the backups? (Choose TWO)

A. Amazon S3
B. Amazon EBS Snapshots
C. Amazon EFS
D. AWS Storage Gateway
E. Amazon ElastiCache

Answer: A, B

---

Question #: 605
A company is implementing a Pilot Light disaster recovery strategy. What are the key components that are typically kept running in the DR region?

A. A fully scaled-out fleet of application servers and a primary database.
B. A small-capacity database instance (the "pilot light") and the application's infrastructure defined in CloudFormation, but with no running application servers.
C. Only the application's AMIs stored in the DR region.
D. A continuously synchronized, hot standby database and a fully scaled-out application fleet.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 606
A company is using a Warm Standby disaster recovery strategy for its web application. What would you expect to find in the DR region?

A. Only backups of the data and infrastructure templates.
B. A scaled-down but fully functional version of the application, running on a smaller fleet of EC2 instances and a smaller database instance.
C. A fully scaled production environment identical to the primary region.
D. A single EC2 instance with the application code ready to be deployed.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 607
Which disaster recovery strategy generally offers the lowest RTO and RPO?

A. Backup and Restore
B. Pilot Light
C. Warm Standby
D. Multi-site Active-Active

Answer: D

---

Question #: 608
A company uses Amazon RDS for its database. They take daily snapshots. In a disaster, they will restore the latest snapshot to a new instance. This process is part of which DR strategy and what does it primarily determine?

A. Pilot Light; it determines the RTO.
B. Backup and Restore; it primarily determines the RTO.
C. Warm Standby; it determines the RPO.
D. Backup and Restore; it primarily determines the RPO.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 609
To automate the deployment of infrastructure in a DR region during a failover event, which AWS service should be used to define the infrastructure as code?

A. AWS Elastic Beanstalk
B. AWS CloudFormation
C. AWS CodeDeploy
D. Amazon EC2 Auto Scaling

Answer: B

---

Question #: 610
What is the primary objective of a Recovery Point Objective (RPO)?

A. To define the maximum duration of a system outage.
B. To define the maximum amount of acceptable data loss.
C. To specify the time it takes to create a backup.
D. To measure the performance of the recovery process.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 611
In a Pilot Light DR strategy, data is often replicated from the primary region to the DR region. For an RDS database, which feature is commonly used to achieve this continuous replication?

A. Manual Snapshots
B. A cross-region Read Replica
C. Automated Backups
D. AWS Database Migration Service (DMS) with change data capture (CDC)

Answer: B

---

Question #: 612
Comparing Pilot Light and Warm Standby, what is the key difference?

A. Pilot Light has a higher cost than Warm Standby.
B. Warm Standby has a running, scaled-down version of the application, while Pilot Light typically does not have running application servers.
C. Pilot Light offers a lower RTO than Warm Standby.
D. Warm Standby does not require data replication, while Pilot Light does.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 613
An application uses an S3 bucket to store critical user documents. To prepare for a regional disaster, what is the simplest way to back up this data to another region?

A. Manually copy the objects every day.
B. Enable versioning on the bucket.
C. Configure S3 Cross-Region Replication (CRR) on the bucket.
D. Take EBS snapshots of the S3 bucket.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 614
Which DNS routing policy in Amazon Route 53 is most commonly used to manually fail over traffic from a primary region to a DR region?

A. Latency-based routing
B. Geolocation routing
C. Weighted routing (by changing the weights to 100 for DR and 0 for primary)
D. Simple routing

Answer: C

---

Question #: 615
What is the primary objective of a Recovery Time Objective (RTO)?

A. To define the frequency of backups.
B. To measure the amount of data lost.
C. To define the maximum acceptable downtime for a system after a disaster.
D. To specify the time it takes to restore a single file.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 616

A. Warm Standby
B. Pilot Light
C. Multi-site Active-Active
D. Backup and Restore

Answer: D

---

Question #: 617
In a Warm Standby DR setup, the application servers in the DR region are running but at a reduced capacity. During a failover, what is the first step that needs to be taken for the application tier?

A. Deploy the application servers from AMIs.
B. Scale out the application servers to handle production load.
C. Restore the application code from S3.
D. Promote the DR database to be the new primary.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 618

C. The ability to copy backups to a different AWS Region
D. Backup lifecycle policies

Answer: C

D. Amazon RDS (in single-AZ mode)

Question #: 620

Answer: A

Question #: 623

Answer: B

---

Question #: 624
What is a key consideration when choosing a DR region?

A. It should be the region with the lowest cost for all services.

Question #: 626

Question #: 627

Question #: 628

A. Pilot Light is generally more expensive because it requires more automation.

D. Pilot Light has higher data transfer costs.

Answer: B

Question #: 629
A company is using AWS Database Migration Service (DMS) to continuously replicate data from an on-premises Oracle database to an RDS for PostgreSQL instance in AWS. How can this setup be part of a DR plan?

A. The RDS instance in AWS can serve as a hot standby for the on-premises database.
B. This setup is only for migration, not DR.
C. The DMS task can be reversed to restore data to the on-premises location.
D. The RDS instance can be used to generate backups for the on-premises database.

Answer: A

Question #: 630

C. Copying files to S3 every hour.

Answer: B

Question #: 631

Question #: 636

C. Only deploying the application servers.

Answer: A

D. Using security groups to restrict access.

Question #: 638

A. Backup and Restore
B. Pilot Light
C. Multi-site Active-Active (where it's used for the initial build)
D. Warm Standby
E. All of the above are enhanced by using CloudFormation.

Answer: E (While most impactful for B&R and Pilot Light, it's a best practice for all).

Question #: 639

A. Yes, because backups are taken daily.
B. No, the RPO is the time to recover, not the data loss.
C. No, a 24-hour RPO means a maximum of 24 hours of data loss, so a daily backup is at the very edge and could exceed it if the disaster happens right before the next backup.

B. Regularly testing the process of restoring from backups to ensure they are valid and meet the RTO.

D. Synchronously replicating data between regions.

SECTION: High-Performance Compute And Storage
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 701

Question #: 702

C. Throughput Optimized HDD (st1)
D. Cold HDD (sc1)

Answer: B

Answer: C

---

Question #: 716
An application requires an EBS volume that can sustain 1,000 IOPS. A 200 GiB gp3 volume is created with the default settings. What needs to be done to meet the IOPS requirement?

A. Nothing, the default IOPS for a 200 GiB gp3 volume is sufficient.
B. The volume must be increased in size to 334 GiB.
C. The IOPS for the gp3 volume must be provisioned to 1,000.
D. A gp3 volume cannot meet this requirement; an io2 volume must be used.

Answer: C (A new gp3 volume defaults to 3,000 IOPS, so a default volume would be sufficient, but the "correct" action to guarantee a specific IOPS number is to provision it).

SECTION: High-Performance Databases
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 801
An e-commerce application is experiencing high read traffic on its main Amazon RDS for MySQL database, causing performance degradation during peak hours. The application can tolerate slightly stale data for product catalog lookups. What is the most effective solution to improve read performance?

A. Enable Multi-AZ on the RDS instance.
B. Increase the instance size of the RDS database.
C. Create an RDS Read Replica and direct all read queries for the product catalog to it.
D. Take more frequent database snapshots.

Answer: C

---

C. Amazon DynamoDB
D. Amazon Redshift

Question #: 824
What is the endpoint used to connect to an Amazon Aurora cluster for read-only queries if you want the load to be distributed across all available Aurora Replicas?

A. The cluster endpoint.
B. The instance endpoint of one of the replicas.
C. The reader endpoint.
D. A custom endpoint.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 825
A DynamoDB Scan operation is being performed on a large table. The operation is consuming a large number of Read Capacity Units and impacting the performance of other critical operations. How can the developer reduce the impact of the Scan operation?

A. Increase the Write Capacity Units (WCUs) of the table.
B. Perform the Scan operation with a smaller `PageSize` and add delays between page requests.
C. Create a Global Secondary Index and scan the index instead.
D. Use a parallel scan.

Answer: B (While parallel scans can be faster, they consume even more capacity. Limiting the scan rate is the way to reduce impact).

---

Question #: 826
Can you create an RDS Read Replica of another Read Replica?

A. Yes, this is called a cascaded read replica.
B. No, a read replica can only be created from a primary source instance.
C. Yes, but only for the MySQL engine.
D. Yes, but only if the source read replica is in a different region.

Answer: B (As of recent updates, some engines like MySQL allow this, but for the exam, the traditional answer is that replicas are created from the primary).

C. `BatchGetItem`
D. `Query`

Answer: D

Question #: 900
An application requires a cache where the most frequently accessed data is kept in memory, but the full dataset (which is larger than memory) is available. This allows for fast access to popular items while still having access to the "long tail" of data. What is this caching pattern called?

A. Write-Through
B. Lazy Loading
C. Cache-Aside
D. This is a primary function of DAX and ElastiCache, acting as a cache in front of a larger database.

Answer: D (The pattern described is the fundamental purpose of a caching layer like ElastiCache or DAX).


SECTION: High-Performance Networking
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 901
A company has a global user base for its web application hosted in a single AWS Region. Users in Asia and Europe are experiencing high latency. The application serves a mix of dynamic and static content. Which service should be used to improve performance for all users by routing them through the AWS global network and caching static content at the edge?

A. S3 Transfer Acceleration
B. AWS Global Accelerator
C. Amazon CloudFront
D. Elastic Load Balancer

Answer: C

Question #: 902

A. Create a VPC peering connection between A and B, B and C, and A and C.

SECTION: High Availability And Scalability

Question #: 1001
A web application experiences heavy traffic during business hours and very little traffic at night. The company wants to ensure they have enough capacity to handle the peak load while minimizing costs during off-peak hours. Which AWS service and feature should be used to automatically adjust the number of EC2 instances?

A. Elastic Load Balancing with sticky sessions
B. Auto Scaling group with a scheduled scaling policy
C. An Amazon CloudWatch alarm that stops instances at night
D. A Multi-AZ deployment for the EC2 instances

Answer: B

---

Question #: 1002

A. It will terminate the unhealthy instance.
B. It will stop routing traffic to the unhealthy instance.
C. It will replace the unhealthy instance with a new one.
D. It will send a notification to the administrator via Amazon SNS.

Question #: 1047
What does it mean for an application to be "stateless"?

A. The application does not require a database.
B. The application does not store any client session data on the server where it is running.
C. The application runs without a traditional operating system.
D. The application does not have a user interface.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 1048
An Auto Scaling group is configured with a minimum size of 2 and a maximum size of 10. There are currently 6 instances running. A scheduled action is configured to set the desired capacity to 8 at 9 AM. What will happen at 9 AM?

A. Two new instances will be launched.
B. Eight new instances will be launched.
C. The maximum size will be changed to 8.
D. Nothing, as the current capacity is within the min/max range.

Answer: A

---

Question #: 1049
The `X-Forwarded-For` header is a feature of which load balancer type that helps identify the original IP address of a client?

A. Network Load Balancer
B. Gateway Load Balancer
C. Application Load Balancer
D. It is a feature of all load balancer types.

Answer: C

Question #: 1050

A. Cross-Region architecture

C. Hybrid cloud architecture
D. On-premises architecture

Answer: B

Question #: 1051

B. Simple Scaling
C. Step Scaling
D. Target Tracking Scaling

Answer: C

Question #: 1052
Can a single Application Load Balancer route traffic to target groups that contain different types of targets, such as EC2 instances and on-premises servers registered by IP address?

A. No, all target groups must contain the same target type.
B. Yes, an ALB can route to different target groups with different target types.
C. No, on-premises servers cannot be targets for an ALB.
D. Yes, but only if the on-premises servers are connected via AWS Direct Connect.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 1053
In a failover scenario for an RDS Multi-AZ instance, what is the typical downtime?

A. It is typically zero, with no interruption to service.
B. It is typically 1 to 2 minutes while the DNS CNAME is flipped to the standby.
C. It is typically 10 to 15 minutes while the standby instance is provisioned.
D. It depends on the size of the database and can take hours.

Answer: B

Question #: 1054
What is the purpose of an instance refresh for an Auto Scaling group?

D. To run a health check on all instances in the group.

Question #: 1055

Question #: 1057

Question #: 1059

C. It will place new instances in the AZ with the lowest latency.

Question #: 1060

Question #: 1061

A. It increases the performance of the database layer.

Question #: 1062

Question #: 1063

Question #: 1064
What is the primary difference between the goals of scalability and elasticity?

A. Scalability is about handling more load by adding resources (scaling up or out), while elasticity is the ability to automatically acquire and release those resources as needed.
B. Scalability is about running in multiple regions, while elasticity is about running in multiple AZs.
C. Scalability refers to databases, while elasticity refers to compute instances.
D. There is no difference; the terms are interchangeable.

Answer: A

Question #: 1065

A. Create a single NAT gateway in one Availability Zone.

Question #: 1077

Question #: 1082

D. They are globally replicated, while Launch Configurations are regional.

Question #: 1085

A. 30 seconds
B. 10 seconds
C. 60 seconds (2 failed checks * 30 seconds apart)
D. 300 seconds (10 successful checks * 30 seconds apart)

Answer: C

---

Question #: 1086

C. `X-Forwarded-Proto`
D. `Host`

Answer: C

Question #: 1087

A. EC2 Health Check
B. ELB Health Check
C. TCP Health Check
D. Custom Health Check

Answer: B

Question #: 1088
Which architectural principle is demonstrated by using an SQS queue to handle requests between a front-end web service and a back-end processing service?

A. Vertical Scaling
B. Tight Coupling
C. Decoupling
D. High Cohesion

Answer: C

Question #: 1089
A company wants to use an Application Load Balancer to serve multiple websites that require different SSL certificates (e.g., `site1.com`, `site2.com`). Which ALB feature allows a single listener to use multiple certificates?

A. Cross-Zone Load Balancing
B. Server Name Indication (SNI)
C. Path-based Routing
D. Sticky Sessions

Answer: B

---

Question #: 1090
If you are designing for high availability, what is the relationship between Availability Zones and AWS Regions?

A. A Region is a collection of Availability Zones.
B. An Availability Zone is a collection of Regions.
C. They are independent of each other.
D. An Availability Zone is another name for a Region.

Answer: A

---

Question #: 1091
An Auto Scaling group has a scale-out alarm on CPU > 70% and a scale-in alarm on CPU < 30%. Both alarms are triggered simultaneously (which is unlikely but possible with metric fluctuations). What happens?

A. The scale-out policy takes precedence to ensure availability.
B. The scale-in policy takes precedence to save costs.
C. Both actions are cancelled out, and no scaling occurs.
D. The Auto Scaling group becomes suspended.

Answer: A

---

Question #: 1092
What is the purpose of connection draining (deregistration delay) on a load balancer?

A. To ensure that an instance is fully booted before receiving traffic.
B. To allow in-flight requests to complete before an instance is removed from service during a scale-in or deployment event.
C. To limit the number of connections an instance can receive.
D. To drain malicious connections from the load balancer.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 1093
A solutions architect needs to improve the read performance of a heavily used RDS database. The application is read-heavy. What is the most effective solution?

A. Enable Multi-AZ on the RDS instance.
B. Increase the size of the RDS instance (scale up).
C. Create one or more Read Replicas and direct read queries to them.
D. Take more frequent database snapshots.

Answer: C

---

Question #: 1094
Which of these is NOT a component of an Auto Scaling group configuration?

A. A launch template or launch configuration.
B. The minimum, maximum, and desired number of instances.
C. A specification of which Availability Zones to use.
D. An IAM role to grant the Auto Scaling group permissions to other services.

Answer: D (The instances launched by the ASG have an IAM role, but the ASG service itself uses a service-linked role created automatically).

---

Question #: 1095
A company wants to distribute incoming traffic to their application between their on-premises data center and their AWS environment. Which AWS service can help achieve this hybrid load balancing?

A. Application Load Balancer
B. AWS Global Accelerator
C. Amazon Route 53 with weighted routing
D. AWS Direct Connect

Answer: C

---

Question #: 1096
If a target group for an Application Load Balancer contains no healthy, registered instances, what will the ALB do with incoming requests?

A. It will return a 503 Service Unavailable error.
B. It will queue the requests until an instance becomes healthy.
C. It will drop the traffic silently.
D. It will redirect the request to a fallback URL.

Answer: A

---

Question #: 1097
Which of the following describes "horizontal scaling" (scaling out)?

A. Increasing the RAM and CPU of an existing server.
B. Adding more servers (instances) to a pool of resources.
C. Upgrading the network connection to a server.
D. Installing a more efficient application on an existing server.

Answer: B

---

Question #: 1098
A company has a stateful application that requires a user to be sent to the same server for every request. They are using a Classic Load Balancer. What feature should they use?

A. Proxy Protocol
B. Cross-Zone Load Balancing
C. Connection Draining
D. Session Affinity (Sticky Sessions)

Answer: D

---

Question #: 1099
A Multi-AZ RDS deployment is primarily designed to improve ________, while a Read Replica is primarily designed to improve ________.

A. availability; performance
B. performance; availability
C. security; cost-effectiveness
D. durability; security

Answer: A

---

Question #: 1100
An Auto Scaling group has a desired capacity of 5. All 5 instances are healthy. An administrator changes the desired capacity to 3. Which policy will the ASG use to determine which 2 instances to terminate?

A. The Health Check Policy
B. The Scaling Policy
C. The Termination Policy
D. The Lifecycle Policy

Answer: C


SECTION: Vpc Network Security Questions
------------------------------------------------------------

Question #: 1101
Which AWS resource acts as a virtual firewall at the instance level to control inbound and outbound traffic?

A. Network ACL
B. Security Group
C. Bastion Host
D. NAT Gateway

Answer: B

Question #: 1102
Which TWO statements are correct about Network ACLs? (Choose TWO)

A. They operate at the subnet level
B. They are stateful
C. They support both allow and deny rules
D. They can only allow traffic
E. They apply at the instance level

Answer: A,C

Question #: 1103
You have a web server in a public subnet that needs to connect to the internet. Which resource must be present in the subnet route table?

A. NAT Gateway
B. Internet Gateway
C. Virtual Private Gateway
D. Security Group

Answer: B

Question #: 1104
Which AWS resource enables instances in a private subnet to access the internet while preventing inbound connections from the internet?

A. Internet Gateway
B. Bastion Host
C. NAT Gateway
D. VPC Peering

Answer: C

Question #: 1105
Which TWO are best practices when using a Bastion Host? (Choose TWO)

A. Place it in a public subnet
B. Use Security Groups to limit SSH access
C. Place it in a private subnet
D. Assign a public IP address
E. Use it for all application traffic

Answer: A,B,D

Question #: 1106
Which is TRUE about Security Groups?

A. They are stateless
B. They evaluate rules in order
C. They only support allow rules
D. They apply at the subnet level

Answer: C

Question #: 1107
What is the main difference between a public and private subnet in AWS?

A. Public subnet has a route to an Internet Gateway
B. Private subnet can never use NAT
C. Private subnet is always more secure
D. Public subnet cannot contain EC2 instances

Answer: A

Question #: 1108
Which TWO statements are correct about NAT Gateways? (Choose TWO)

A. They support inbound connections from the internet
B. They are used by private subnets to access the internet
C. They must be deployed in a public subnet
D. They replace Security Groups
E. They provide DNS resolution for VPCs

Answer: B,C

A. VPN Connection
B. VPC Endpoint
C. VPC Peering
D. Transit Gateway

Answer: C

A. VPN Connection
B. VPC Endpoint
C. VPC Peering
D. Transit Gateway

Answer: C

Question #: 1140
You need to securely manage EC2 instances in private subnets. Which resource should you deploy?

A. Internet Gateway
B. NAT Gateway
C. Bastion Host
D. Network ACL

Answer: C

Question #: 1141
Which AWS resource acts as a virtual firewall at the instance level to control inbound and outbound traffic?

A. Network ACL
B. Security Group
C. Bastion Host
D. NAT Gateway

Answer: B

Question #: 1142
Which TWO statements are correct about Network ACLs? (Choose TWO)

A. They operate at the subnet level
B. They are stateful
C. They support both allow and deny rules
D. They can only allow traffic
E. They apply at the instance level

Answer: A,C

Question #: 1143
You have a web server in a public subnet that needs to connect to the internet. Which resource must be present in the subnet route table?

A. NAT Gateway
B. Internet Gateway
C. Virtual Private Gateway
D. Security Group

Answer: B

Question #: 1144
Which AWS resource enables instances in a private subnet to access the internet while preventing inbound connections from the internet?

A. Internet Gateway
B. Bastion Host
C. NAT Gateway
D. VPC Peering

Answer: C

Question #: 1145
Which TWO are best practices when using a Bastion Host? (Choose TWO)

A. Place it in a public subnet
B. Use Security Groups to limit SSH access
C. Place it in a private subnet
D. Assign a public IP address
E. Use it for all application traffic

Answer: A,B,D

Question #: 1146
Which is TRUE about Security Groups?

A. They are stateless
B. They evaluate rules in order
C. They only support allow rules
D. They apply at the subnet level

Answer: C

Question #: 1147
What is the main difference between a public and private subnet in AWS?

A. Public subnet has a route to an Internet Gateway
B. Private subnet can never use NAT
C. Private subnet is always more secure
D. Public subnet cannot contain EC2 instances

Answer: A

Question #: 1148
Which TWO statements are correct about NAT Gateways? (Choose TWO)

A. They support inbound connections from the internet
B. They are used by private subnets to access the internet
C. They must be deployed in a public subnet
D. They replace Security Groups
E. They provide DNS resolution for VPCs

Answer: B,C

Question #: 1149
Which AWS feature allows connecting VPCs across accounts and regions privately?

A. VPN Connection
B. VPC Endpoint
C. VPC Peering
D. Transit Gateway

Answer: C
